```
       xy = as.double(xy), d = as.double(d), alpha = as.double(alpha0), 
       mu = as.double(mu0), Xr = as.double(Xr0), S = as.integer(S - 
           1), DUP = FALSE)
DUP is no longer supported and will be ignored.
```
```
DONE
Status: 1 NOTE
```
